<p>Despite
their
worldwide
popularity,
the
band
has
remained
protective
of
how
their
music
is
used
in
the
media,
refusing
its
use
for
<a
href="/wiki/Product_endorsement?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Product
endorsement"
class="mw-redirect">product
endorsements</a>.
In
the
past,
Coldplay
turned
down
multi-million
dollar
contracts
from
<a
href="/wiki/Gatorade?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Gatorade">Gatorade</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Diet_Coke?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Diet
Coke">Diet
Coke</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Gap_Inc.?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Gap
Inc.">Gap</a>,
who
wanted
to
use
the
songs
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Yellow_(Coldplay_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Yellow
(Coldplay
song)">Yellow</a>&quot;,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Trouble_(Coldplay_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Trouble
(Coldplay
song)">Trouble</a>&quot;,
and
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Don%27t_Panic_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Don't
Panic
(song)">Don't
Panic</a>&quot;
respectively.<sup
id="cite_ref-ETP_153-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-ETP-153"><span>[</span>153<span>]</span></a></sup>
According
to
frontman,
Chris
Martin,
&quot;We
wouldn't
be
able
to
live
with
ourselves
if
we
sold
the
songs'
meanings
like
that.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-ETP_153-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-ETP-153"><span>[</span>153<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
song
&quot;Viva
la
Vida&quot;
was
featured
in
a
commercial
for
the
<a
href="/wiki/ITunes_Store?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="ITunes
Store">iTunes
Store</a>,
advertising
its
exclusive
availability
of
the
single
as
a
digital
download
on
<a
href="/wiki/ITunes?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="ITunes">iTunes</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-154"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-154"><span>[</span>154<span>]</span></a></sup>
Additionally,
Chris
Martin
appeared
at
an
<a
href="/wiki/Apple_Inc.?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Apple
Inc.">Apple
Inc.</a>
Special
Event
on
1
September
2010,
playing
a
number
of
songs,
and
also
thanked
Apple
for
their
assistance
in
marketing
&quot;Viva
la
Vida&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-155"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-155"><span>[</span>155<span>]</span></a></sup>
After
the
death
of
<a
href="/wiki/Steve_Jobs?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Steve
Jobs">Steve
Jobs</a>,
Coldplay
performed
four
songs
at
Apple's
Campus
in
Cupertino,
further
thanking
Jobs
for
the
support
he
gave
them.<sup
id="cite_ref-156"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Coldplay
supports
<a
href="/wiki/Amnesty_International?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Amnesty
International">Amnesty
International</a>
and
performed
for
them
at
<a
href="/wiki/The_Secret_Policeman%27s_Ball_2012?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Secret
Policeman's
Ball
2012">The
Secret
Policeman's
Ball</a>
fundraiser
in
2012.<sup
id="cite_ref-roach_78_157-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-roach_78-157"><span>[</span>157<span>]</span></a></sup>
Martin
is
regarded
as
one
of
the
most
visible
celebrity
advocates
for
<a
href="/wiki/Fair_trade?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Fair
trade">fair
trade</a>,
supporting
<a
href="/wiki/Oxfam?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Oxfam">Oxfam</a>'s
ongoing
<a
href="/wiki/Make_Trade_Fair?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Make
Trade
Fair">Make
Trade
Fair</a>
campaign.<sup
id="cite_ref-158"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-158"><span>[</span>158<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
has
been
on
trips
with
Oxfam
to
assess
conditions,
has
appeared
in
its
advertising
campaign,
and
is
known
for
wearing
a
&quot;Make
Trade
Fair&quot;
wristband
during
public
appearances
(including
at
Coldplay
concerts).<sup
id="cite_ref-159"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-159"><span>[</span>159<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
band
were
also
filmed
for
<a
href="/wiki/Make_Poverty_History?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Make
Poverty
History">Make
Poverty
History</a>,
clicking
their
fingers.<sup
id="cite_ref-160"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-160"><span>[</span>160<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>During
the
early
years,
Coldplay
became
widely
known
in
the
media
for
giving
10
percent
of
the
band's
profits
to
charity,<sup
id="cite_ref-161"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-161"><span>[</span>161<span>]</span></a></sup>
which
they
continue
to
do.<sup
id="cite_ref-162"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-162"><span>[</span>162<span>]</span></a></sup>
Bassist
Guy
Berryman
said,
&quot;You
can
make
people
aware
of
issues.
It
isn't
very
much
effort
for
us
at
all,
but
if
it
can
help
people,
then
we
want
to
do
it.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-roach_78_157-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-roach_78-157"><span>[</span>157<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
band
also
asks
that
any
gifts
intended
for
them
are
donated
to
charity,
according
to
a
response
on
the
FAQ
section
of
Coldplay's
website.
Martin
<a
href="/wiki/Opposition_to_the_Iraq_War?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Opposition
to
the
Iraq
War">spoke
out
against</a>
the
<a
href="/wiki/2003_invasion_of_Iraq?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="2003
invasion
of
Iraq">2003
invasion
of
Iraq</a>
by
the
US,
UK
and
other
forces,
and
endorsed
the
US
<a
href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Democratic
Party
(United
States)">Democratic</a>
presidential
candidates
<a
href="/wiki/John_Kerry?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="John
Kerry">John
Kerry</a><sup
id="cite_ref-163"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-163"><span>[</span>163<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Barack_Obama?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Barack
Obama">Barack
Obama</a>
in
2004
and
2008
respectively.<sup
id="cite_ref-164"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-164"><span>[</span>164<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
June
2009,
Coldplay
began
supporting
Meat
Free
Monday,
a
food
campaign
started
by
<a
href="/wiki/Paul_McCartney?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Paul
McCartney">Paul
McCartney</a>
which
attempts
to
help
slow
climate
change
by
having
at
least
one
meat
free
day
a
week.<sup
id="cite_ref-165"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-165"><span>[</span>165<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>From
17
and
31
December
2009,
Coldplay
auctioned
a
quantity
of
significant
band
memorabilia,
including
their
first
guitars.
Proceeds
went
to
<a
href="/wiki/Kids_Company?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kids
Company">Kids
Company</a>,
a
charity
which
helps
vulnerable
children
and
young
people
in
London.<sup
id="cite_ref-166"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-166"><span>[</span>166<span>]</span></a></sup>
A
month
later
in
January
2010,
Coldplay
performed
a
slightly
modified
version
of
&quot;A
Message&quot;,
entitled
&quot;A
Message
2010&quot;,
at
the
Hope
For
Haiti
Now
telethon
special,
raising
money
for
the
victims
of
the
<a
href="/wiki/2010_Haiti_earthquake?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="2010
Haiti
earthquake">2010
Haiti
earthquake</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-167"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-167"><span>[</span>167<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
2011
Coldplay
endorsed
the
song
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Freedom_for_Palestine?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Freedom
for
Palestine">Freedom
for
Palestine</a>&quot;
by
posting
a
link
to
the
video.
In
less
than
a
day
12,000
comments
were
made
on
that
post.
Some
threatened
to
boycott
the
band,
and
a
Facebook
group
was
created
that
demanded
an
apology
to
Israel.<sup
id="cite_ref-168"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-168"><span>[</span>168<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
link
to
the
song
was
eventually
removed
from
their
Facebook
wall.<sup
id="cite_ref-169"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-169"><span>[</span>169<span>]</span></a></sup>
According
to
Frank
Barat
of
OneWorld,
the
link
was
not
removed
by
Coldplay,
but
by
Facebook
after
&quot;thousands
of
people
(and
computer
generated
posts)
reported
it
as
abusive.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-170"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-170"><span>[</span>170<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Album
Artists
(www.albumartists.co.uk)
staged
an
exhibition
of
art
from
<i>Mylo
Xyloto</i>
at
Proud
Gallery
in
<a
href="/wiki/Camden_Town?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Camden
Town">Camden</a>
to
support
the
charity
<a
href="/wiki/Kids_Company?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kids
Company">Kids
Company</a>
in
Novemberâ€”December
2012.<sup
id="cite_ref-171"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-171"><span>[</span>171<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
exhibition
raised
over
&pound;610,000
for
the
children's
charity
which
supports
disadvantaged
children
in
London.<sup
id="cite_ref-172"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-172"><span>[</span>172<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Awards_and_nominations">Awards
and
nominations</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Coldplay&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14"
title="Edit
section:
Awards
and
nominations">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<ul>









<li><i>Main
article:
<a
href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Coldplay?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="List
of

and
nominations

of

</ul>








<p>Coldplay
has
<a
href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Coldplay?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="List
of
awards
and
nominations
received
by
Coldplay">won
numerous
music
awards</a>
throughout
their
history,
including
eight
<a
href="/wiki/Brit_Award?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Brit
Award"
class="mw-redirect">Brit
Awards</a>â€”winning
Best
British
Group
three
times,
five
<a
href="/wiki/MTV_Video_Music_Award?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="MTV
Video
Music
Award">MTV
Video
Music
Awards</a>,
three
<a
href="/wiki/World_Music_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="World
Music
Awards">World
Music
Awards</a>,
four
<a
href="/wiki/Billboard_Music_Award?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Billboard
Music
Award">Billboard
Music
Awards</a>,
and
seven
<a
href="/wiki/Grammy_Award?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Grammy
Award">Grammy
Awards</a>
out
of
twenty
six
nominations.
2009
was
their
most
successful
year
having
received
seven
Grammy
Award
nominations
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/51st_Grammy_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="51st
Grammy
Awards"
class="mw-redirect">51st
Grammy
Awards</a>,
and
won
three.<sup
id="cite_ref-174"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-174"><span>[</span>174<span>]</span></a></sup>
Coldplay
have
sold
over
60
million
records
worldwide.<sup
id="cite_ref-Independent2012_10-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Independent2012-10"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-Bloomberg2012_11-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Bloomberg2012-11"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Coldplay&page=1&ac=24&qid=7DEDA37663A88AA37DFADBB07F2B9C8A&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>
